  function readCookieL(c_name) {
      if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
          c_start = document.cookie.indexOf(c_name + "=");
          if (c_start != -1) {
              c_start = c_start + c_name.length + 1;
              c_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", c_start);
              if (c_end == -1) {
                  c_end = document.cookie.length;
              }
              return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start, c_end));
          }
      }
      return "";
  }

                var number = Number(value);
                if (isNaN(number)) { return 0; }
                if (number === 0 || !isFinite(number)) { return number; }

        addEventListener: function addEventListener(type, listener, options, element) {
            try {
                if (typeof element == "undefined") {
                    element = document;
                }

                if (typeof options == "undefined") {
                    options = false;
                }

                element.addEventListener ? element.addEventListener(type, listener, options) : element.attachEvent && element.attachEvent("on" + type, listener);
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e.message);
            }
        },
        removeEventListener: function addEventListener(type, event, listener, element) {
            try {
                if (typeof element == "undefined") {
                    element = document;
                }

                element.removeEventListener ? element.removeEventListener(event, listener):null;
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e.message);
            }
        },
        isInViewport: function isInViewport(elem) {
            try {
                var bounding = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
                var windowInnerHeight = sozcuCommon.innerHeight();
                var windowInnerWidth = sozcuCommon.innerWidth();

                if (bounding.top < windowInnerHeight && bounding.bottom > 0 && bounding.left < windowInnerWidth && bounding.right > 0) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            } catch (err) {
                return false;
            }
        },
        querySelector: function querySelector(selector, node) {
            if (typeof document.querySelector == "undefined") return null;

            if (!node) {
                node = document;
            }

            return node.querySelector(selector);
        },
        querySelectorAll: function querySelectorAll(selector, node) {
            if (typeof document.querySelectorAll == "undefined") return [];

            if (!node) {
                node = document;
            }

            return node.querySelectorAll(selector);
        },
        generateQuerySelector: function(el) {
            var path = [], parent, pathJoin;

            while (parent = el.parentNode) {
                var tag = el.tagName, siblings;
                path.unshift(
                    (
                        siblings = parent.children,
                            [].filter.call(siblings, function(sibling){return sibling.tagName === tag}).length === 1 ? tag :
                                tag + ":nth-child(" + (1 + [].indexOf.call(siblings, el))+ ")"
                    )
                );
                el = parent;
            };

            pathJoin = path.join(' > ');
            return pathJoin.toLowerCase();
        },
        isDomObjectCloseToView: function isDomObjectCloseToView(domObject, threshold) {
            var viewBottom = sozcuCommon.pageYOffset() + sozcuCommon.innerHeight() + threshold;
            var bounding = domObject.getBoundingClientRect();

            if (bounding.top < viewBottom) {
                return true;
            }

            return false;
        },
        cloneSO: function cloneSO(obj) {
            // Handle the 3 simple types, and null or undefined
            if (null == obj || "object" != _typeof(obj)) return obj; // Handle Date

            if (_instanceof(obj, Date)) {
                var copy = new Date();
                copy.setTime(obj.getTime());
                return copy;
            } // Handle Array


            if (_instanceof(obj, Array)) {
                var copy = [];

                for (var i = 0, len = obj.length; i < len; i++) {
                    copy[i] = sozcuCommon.cloneSO(obj[i]);
                }

                return copy;
            } // Handle Object


            if (_instanceof(obj, Object)) {
                var copy = {};

                for (var attr in obj) {
                    if (obj.hasOwnProperty(attr)) copy[attr] = sozcuCommon.cloneSO(obj[attr]);
                }

                return copy;
            }

            throw new Error("Unable to copy obj! Its type isn't supported.");
        },
        closestByClass: function closestByClass(el, clazz) {
            // Traverse the DOM up with a while loop
            while (el.className != clazz) {
                // Increment the loop to the parent node
                el = el.parentNode;

                if (!el) {
                    return null;
                }
            } // At this point, the while loop has stopped and `el` represents the element that has
            // the class you specified in the second parameter of the function `clazz`
            // Then return the matched element


            return el;
        },
        changePageUrl: function changePageUrl(newUrl) {
            if (window.location.origin + window.location.pathname == newUrl) {
                return false;
            }

            var isIE = sozcuCommon.isBrowserIE();

            if (!isIE) {
                window.history.replaceState("state", "title", newUrl);
            } else if (isIE > 9) {
                window.history.replaceState("state", "title", newUrl);
            }

            sozcuContent.onPageUrlChanged();
            sozcuDFP.onPageUrlChanged();


            sozcuCommon.urlChangeCount++;
        },
        isBrowserIE: function isBrowserIE() {
            var myNav = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
            return myNav.indexOf('msie') != -1 ? parseInt(myNav.split('msie')[1]) : false;
        },
        errorHandler: function errorHandler(error) {
            //console.log(arguments);
            return true;
        },
        ajaxGet: function ajaxGet(url, successFunction, errorFunction) {
            var xmlHttpRequest = window.XMLHttpRequest;
            if (!xmlHttpRequest) return sozcuCommon.errorHandler('window XMLHttpRequest object not exist!'), false;
            var xmlHttpRequestObject = new xmlHttpRequest();
            if (!("withCredentials" in xmlHttpRequestObject)) return sozcuCommon.errorHandler('window XMLHttpRequest object  has not withCredentials property!'), false;
            xmlHttpRequestObject.open("GET", url, true);
            xmlHttpRequestObject.withCredentials = false;
            xmlHttpRequestObject.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");

            xmlHttpRequestObject.onload = function () {
                if (4 == xmlHttpRequestObject.readyState) {
                    try {
                        sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer && clearTimeout(sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer);

                        if (200 != xmlHttpRequestObject.status) {
                            errorFunction && errorFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject);
                            sozcuCommon.errorHandler("Ajax call failed", {
                                xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                            });
                        } else {
                            successFunction && successFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject.responseText);
                        }
                    } catch (err) {
                        sozcuCommon.errorHandler(err.message, {
                            err: err,
                            xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                        });
                        return false;
                    }

                    xmlHttpRequestObject = null;
                }
            };

            xmlHttpRequestObject.send();
            sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                errorFunction && errorFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject);
                sozcuCommon.errorHandler("Ajax call timeout", {
                    xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                });
            }, 5000);
            return true;
        },
        ajaxPost: function ajaxPost(url, data, successFunction, errorFunction) {
            var xmlHttpRequest = window.XMLHttpRequest;
            if (!xmlHttpRequest) return sozcuCommon.errorHandler('window XMLHttpRequest object not exist!'), false;
            var xmlHttpRequestObject = new xmlHttpRequest();
            if (!("withCredentials" in xmlHttpRequestObject)) return sozcuCommon.errorHandler('window XMLHttpRequest object  has not withCredentials property!'), false;
            xmlHttpRequestObject.open("POST", url, true);
            xmlHttpRequestObject.withCredentials = true;
            xmlHttpRequestObject.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");

            xmlHttpRequestObject.onload = function () {
                if (4 == xmlHttpRequestObject.readyState) {
                    try {
                        sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer && clearTimeout(sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer);

                        if (200 != xmlHttpRequestObject.status) {
                            errorFunction && errorFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject);
                            sozcuCommon.errorHandler("Ajax call failed", {
                                xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                            });
                        } else {
                            successFunction && successFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject.responseText);
                        }
                    } catch (err) {
                        sozcuCommon.errorHandler(err.message, {
                            err: err,
                            xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                        });
                        return false;
                    }

                    xmlHttpRequestObject = null;
                }
            };

            xmlHttpRequestObject.send(data);
            sozcuCommon.ajaxPostTimer = setTimeout(function () {
                errorFunction && errorFunction(xmlHttpRequestObject);
                sozcuCommon.errorHandler("Ajax call timeout", {
                    xmlHttpRequestObject: xmlHttpRequestObject
                });
            }, 5000);
            return true;
        },
        ajaxJsonPost: function ajaxJsonPost(url, data, successFunction, errorFunction) {
            if (!window.JSON) return sozcuCommon.errorHandler('window JSON object not exist!'), false;
            return sozcuCommon.ajaxPost(url, JSON.stringify(data), successFunction, errorFunction);
        },
        isMobile: function isMobile() {
            var isMobile = /iPhone|iPod|Android|Windows Phone/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
            return isMobile;
        },
        readCookie: function readCookie(name) {
            var start = document.cookie.indexOf(name + "=");

            if (start != -1) {
                start = start + name.length + 1;
                var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", start);

                if (end == -1) {
                    end = document.cookie.length;
                }

                return document.cookie.substring(start, end);
            }

            return null;
        },
        unescapeReadCookie: function unescapeReadCookie(c_name) {
            if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
                c_start = document.cookie.indexOf(c_name + "=");
                if (c_start != -1) {
                    c_start = c_start + c_name.length + 1;
                    c_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", c_start);
                    if (c_end == -1) {
                        c_end = document.cookie.length;
                    }
                    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start, c_end));
                }
            }
            return "";
        },
        createCookie: function createCookie(name, value, days) {
            var expires;
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
            expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
            document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
        },
        removeCookie: function removeCookie(name) {
            sozcuCommon.createCookie(name, "", -1);
        },
        findParentElement: function findParentElement(tagName, el) {
            while (el) {
                if ((el.nodeName || el.tagName).toLowerCase() === tagName.toLowerCase()) {
                    return el;
                }

                el = el.parentNode;
            }

            return null;
        },
        parseURL: function parseURL(url) {
            var parsed_url = {};
            if (url == null || url.length == 0) return parsed_url;
            protocol_i = url.indexOf('://');
            parsed_url.protocol = url.substr(0, protocol_i);
            remaining_url = url.substr(protocol_i + 3, url.length);
            domain_i = remaining_url.indexOf('/');
            domain_i = domain_i == -1 ? remaining_url.length - 1 : domain_i;
            parsed_url.domain = remaining_url.substr(0, domain_i);
            parsed_url.path = domain_i == -1 || domain_i + 1 == remaining_url.length ? null : remaining_url.substr(domain_i + 1, remaining_url.length);
            domain_parts = parsed_url.domain.split('.');

            switch (domain_parts.length) {
                case 2:
                    parsed_url.subdomain = null;
                    parsed_url.host = domain_parts[0];
                    parsed_url.tld = domain_parts[1];
                    break;

                case 3:
                    parsed_url.subdomain = domain_parts[0];
                    parsed_url.host = domain_parts[1];
                    parsed_url.tld = domain_parts[2];
                    break;

                case 4:
                    parsed_url.subdomain = domain_parts[0];
                    parsed_url.host = domain_parts[1];
                    parsed_url.tld = domain_parts[2] + '.' + domain_parts[3];
                    break;
            }

            parsed_url.parent_domain = parsed_url.host + '.' + parsed_url.tld;
            return parsed_url;
        },
        parseURL2: function(url){

            var parser = document.createElement('a') ,
                searchObject = {},
                queries, split, i;
            // Let the browser do the work
            parser.href = url;
            // Convert query string to object
            queries = parser.search.replace(/^\?/, '').split('&');
            for( i = 0; i < queries.length; i++ ) {
                split = queries[i].split('=');
                searchObject[split[0]] = split[1];
            }

            return {
                protocol: parser.protocol,
                host: parser.host,
                hostname: parser.hostname,
                port: parser.port,
                pathname: parser.pathname,
                search: parser.search,
                searchObject: searchObject,
                hash: parser.hash
            };
        },
        getCanonicalUrl: function(){
            var canonicalUrl = "";
            var link = sozcuCommon.querySelector("link[rel='canonical']");
            if (link){
                canonicalUrl = link.getAttribute("href");
            }

            return canonicalUrl;
        },

            return window.location.href;
        },

        log: function(log){
            if(jsHelper.debugMode &&
                typeof window.console != 'undefined'
            ) {
                console.log(log);
            }

        ltrim: function (str, char) {
            if(typeof char == 'undefined'){
                char = " ";
            }
            if (str.slice(0, char.length) === char) {
                return this.ltrim(str.slice(char.length), char);
            } else {
                return str;
            }
        },
        rtrim: function (str, char) {
            if(typeof char == 'undefined'){
                char = " ";
            }
            if (str.slice(str.length - char.length) === char) {
                return this.rtrim(str.slice(0, 0 - char.length), char);
            } else {
                return str;
            }
        },
        trim: function (str, char) {
            if(typeof char == 'undefined'){
                char = " ";
            }
            return this.ltrim(this.rtrim(str, char), char);
        },
        addReadArticle: function (articleId){
            articleId = String(articleId);
            var arr = [];
            var knt = 0;
            if (sozcuCommon.readCookie(varReadCookie) !== null) {
                arr = sozcuCommon.readCookie(varReadCookie).split(',');
                if(arr.length > 49){
                    // remember only 50 news
                    arr = [];
                }
                if (arr.indexOf(articleId)===-1){
                    arr.push(articleId);
                    knt = 1;
                }
            }else{
                arr.push(articleId);
                knt = 1;
            }


            if (knt === 1){
                sozcuCommon.createCookie(varReadCookie, arr, 1);
            }
        },
        isArticleRead: function (articleId){
            var isRead = false;
            if(sozcuCommon.readCookie(varReadCookie) !== null){
                arr = [];
                sozcuCommon.readCookie(varReadCookie).split(',').forEach(function(cv,ck) {
                    arr.push(cv);
                });
                if(arr.indexOf(articleId) !== -1){
                    isRead = true;
                }
            }

            return isRead;
        }, emptyArticleRead: function (){
            sozcuCommon.removeCookie(varReadCookie);
        }
    };

    var sozcuDFP = {
        lockGDPR: true,
        slots: {},
        active: true,
        targetingList: {},
        firstInitialized: false,
        scrollEventListenerInit: false,
        scrollEventListenerTimeoutRefresh: null,
        scrollEventListenerTimeoutAutoRefresh: null,
        scrollEventListenerTimeoutSticky: null,
        lockGDPRInterval: {},
        lockGDPRPrebidInterval: {},
        stickyDoneInterval: null,
        stickyControlIntervalAdvDisplayed: {},
        stickyControlIntervalViewPort: {},
        onPageUrlChanged: function onPageUrlChanged() {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                googletag.pubads().updateCorrelator();
            });

            Object.keys(sozcuDFP.slots).forEach(function (key) {
                var slot = sozcuDFP.slots[key];

                if (slot.active && slot.refreshWhenPageUrlChanged) {
                    slot.clearAutoRefreshInterval();
                    sozcuDFP.runSlot(slot, true);
                }
            });
        },
        getSlot: function getSlot(divId) {
            return sozcuDFP.slots[divId];
        },
        addSlot: function addSlot(sozcuDFPSlot) {
            var valid = true;

            if (!sozcuDFPSlot.adUnitPath) {
                valid = false;
                console.log("adUnitPath not defined");
            }

            if (!sozcuDFPSlot.divId) {
                valid = false;
                console.log("divId not defined");
            }

            if (valid) {
                sozcuDFP.slots[sozcuDFPSlot.divId] = sozcuDFPSlot;
            } else {
                console.log("DFP slot not added!");
                console.log(sozcuDFPSlot);
            }
        },
        updateSlot: function updateSlot(sozcuDFPSlot) {
            sozcuDFP.addSlot(sozcuDFPSlot);
        },
        getSozcuDFPSlot: function getSozcuDFPSlot() {
            return sozcuCommon.cloneSO(sozcuDFPSlot);
        },
        init: function init() {
            if (sozcuDFP.firstInitialized == false) {
                sozcuDFP.firstInitialized = true;
                sozcuDFP.defineTargeting();
                sozcuDFP.defineSlotRenderEnded();
                sozcuDFP.enableServices();
                sozcuDFP.intiAutoRefresh();
            }

            sozcuDFP.initRefresh();
            sozcuDFP.initSticky();
        },
        initRefresh: function initRefresh() {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            var prebidAddUnits = [];
            Object.keys(sozcuDFP.slots).forEach(function (key) {
                var slot = sozcuDFP.slots[key];

                if (slot.active && slot.initRefresh == false) {
                    sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setInitRefresh(true));

                    if(!slot.lazyLoad){
                        if (!slot.initSlotDefined) {
                            sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setInitSlotDefined(true));
                            sozcuDFP.defineSlot(slot);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });


            // lazyload
            if (sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerInit == false) {
                sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerInit = true;
                sozcuCommon.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
                    sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutRefresh && clearTimeout(sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutRefresh);
                    sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutRefresh = setTimeout(function () {
                        Object.keys(sozcuDFP.slots).forEach(function (key) {
                            var slot = sozcuDFP.slots[key];

                            if (slot.active && slot.lazyLoad && !slot.refreshed) {
                                var slotDomObject = sozcuCommon.querySelector("#" + slot.divId);

                                if (slotDomObject && sozcuCommon.isDomObjectCloseToView(slotDomObject.parentNode, sozcuDFPConstants.thresholdCloseToViewPort)) {

                                    if (!slot.initSlotDefined) {
                                        sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setInitSlotDefined(true));
                                        sozcuDFP.defineSlot(slot);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }, 50);
                });
            }
        },
        intiAutoRefresh: function intiAutoRefresh() {
            var autoRefreshFunction = function autoRefreshFunction() {
                sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutAutoRefresh && clearTimeout(sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutAutoRefresh);
                sozcuDFP.scrollEventListenerTimeoutAutoRefresh = setTimeout(function () {
                    Object.keys(sozcuDFP.slots).forEach(function (key) {
                        var slot = sozcuDFP.slots[key];

                        if (slot.active && slot.autoRefresh) {
                            if (!slot.autoRefreshInterval) {
                                var domElement = sozcuCommon.querySelector("#" + slot.divId);

                                if (sozcuCommon.isInViewport(domElement)) {
                                    slot.autoRefreshInterval = setInterval(function (slot) {
                                        var domElement = sozcuCommon.querySelector("#" + slot.divId);

                                        if (sozcuCommon.isInViewport(domElement)) {
                                            if (slot.refreshTime && slot.refreshTime + sozcuDFPConstants.autoRefreshTime <= 1 * new Date()) {
                                                sozcuDFP.runSlot(slot, true);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            slot.autoRefreshInterval && clearInterval(slot.autoRefreshInterval);
                                        }

                                        sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setAutoRefreshInterval(null));
                                    }, sozcuDFPConstants.autoRefreshTime, slot);
                                    sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, 300);
            };

            sozcuCommon.addEventListener("scroll", autoRefreshFunction);
            autoRefreshFunction();
        },
        initSticky: function initSticky() {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            var stickyControl = function stickyControl() {

                sozcuCommon.querySelectorAll('.masthead').forEach(function (node) {
                    //var addSticky = sozcuCommon.closestByClass(node, 'masthead');
                    var addSticky = node;

                    if (node && !node.classList.contains('sticky-done')) {

                        //var addStickyBoundingClientRect = addSticky.getBoundingClientRect();
                        if(!node.classList.contains('sticky-object') && location.href.indexOf('ilan-2') == -1){
                            node.classList.add('sticky-object');
                        }
                        // if (sozcuCommon.pageYOffset() > addStickyBoundingClientRect.top + sozcuDFPConstants.addStickyTopOffset) {
                        //     stickyCount(addSticky);
                        // } else

                        //
                        var stickyKey = sozcuCommon.md5(sozcuCommon.generateQuerySelector(node));

                        (sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalViewPort[stickyKey] && clearInterval(sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalViewPort[stickyKey]));

                        sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalViewPort[stickyKey] =  setInterval(function (node, stickyKey) {


                            if (sozcuCommon.isInViewport(node.firstElementChild)) {
                                clearInterval(sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalViewPort[stickyKey]);
                                (sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalAdvDisplayed[stickyKey] && clearInterval(sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalAdvDisplayed[stickyKey]));
                                sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalAdvDisplayed[stickyKey] =  setInterval(function (node, stickyKey) {
                                    if(sozcuCommon.querySelector('.adv-displayed', node)){
                                        clearInterval(sozcuDFP.stickyControlIntervalAdvDisplayed[stickyKey]);
                                        node.classList.add('display-counting');
                                        setTimeout(function (node) {
                                            node.classList.remove('sticky-object');
                                            node.classList.remove('display-counting');
                                            node.classList.add('sticky-done');
                                        }, 3000, node);
                                    }
                                }, 100, node, stickyKey);

                            }

                        }, 300, node, stickyKey);
                    }
                });
            };

            if(sozcuCommon.isMobile() == false) {
                if (document.readyState === "complete"
                    || document.readyState === "loaded"
                    || document.readyState === "interactive"){
                    stickyControl();
                } else {
                    sozcuCommon.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
                        stickyControl();
                    }, false, window);
                }
            }
        },
        googleTagRefresh: function googleTagRefresh(slot) {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            if (slot && slot.slotObject) {
                sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setRefreshed(true));

                if(
                    typeof sozcuDFP.lockGDPRInterval[slot.divId] == "undefined"
                    || sozcuDFP.lockGDPRInterval[slot.divId] == null
                ) {
                    sozcuDFP.lockGDPRInterval[slot.divId] = setInterval(function (slot) {
                        if (!sozcuDFP.lockGDPR) {
                            clearInterval(sozcuDFP.lockGDPRInterval[slot.divId]);
                            sozcuDFP.lockGDPRInterval[slot.divId] = null
                            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                                sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setRefreshTime(1 * new Date())); //console.log("Refreshed " + slot.divId + " - " + slot.adUnitPath);
                                googletag.pubads().refresh([slot.slotObject], {
                                    changeCorrelator: false
                                });
                            });
                        }
                    }, 10, slot);
                }
            }
        },
        runSlot: function (slot, refreshForce){
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            if (typeof refreshForce == "undefined") {
                refreshForce = false;
            }

            if (!slot.initSlotDefined) {
                sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setInitSlotDefined(true));
                sozcuDFP.defineSlot(slot);
            } else {
                if (slot.prebidActive && slot.prebidData) {
                    sozcuDFP.addPrebidAddUnits([slot], refreshForce);
                } else  {
                    sozcuDFP.refreshFunction(slot, refreshForce);
                }
            }
        },
        refreshFunction: function refreshFunction(slot, refreshForce) {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            if (typeof refreshForce == "undefined") {
                refreshForce = false;
            }

            if (slot.active) {

                if (slot.slotObject) {

                    sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setRefreshed(true));

                    if (!slot.initDisplayScript && slot.interstitial == false) {
                        var domObject = sozcuCommon.querySelector('#' + slot.divId);

                        if (domObject) {
                            domObject.innerHTML = sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayScript(slot.divId);
                        }
                    } // (once in 5 try at private window) some how dfpDisplayScript not getting active before refresh thats why we are putting setTimeout 5 milliseconds


                    setTimeout(function () {
                        if (refreshForce) {
                            sozcuDFP.googleTagRefresh(slot);
                        } else if (!slot.refresh) {
                            sozcuDFP.googleTagRefresh(slot);
                        }
                    }, 5);
                }
            }
        },
        defineSlot: function defineSlot(slot) {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }

            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                var slotObject = null;
                if (slot.interstitial) {
                    slotObject = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(slot.adUnitPath, googletag.enums.OutOfPageFormat.INTERSTITIAL);
                } else if (slot.sizes) {
                    slotObject = googletag.defineSlot(slot.adUnitPath, slot.sizes, slot.divId);
                } else {
                    slotObject = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(slot.adUnitPath, slot.divId);
                }

                if(!slotObject){
                    sozcuCommon.log("slotObject not found for "+ slot.adUnitPath);
                }

                if (slot.sizeMappings && slot.sizeMappings.length > 0) {
                    var sizeMapping = googletag.sizeMapping();
                    slot.sizeMappings.forEach(function (sizes) {
                        if (sizes.length > 1) {
                            sizeMapping.addSize(sizes[0], sizes[1]);
                        }
                    });

                    if(slotObject) {
                        slotObject.defineSizeMapping(sizeMapping.build());
                    }
                }

                if (slotObject && slot.collapseEmptyDiv) {
                    if (slot.collapseEmptyDiv.length > 1) {
                        slotObject.setCollapseEmptyDiv(slot.collapseEmptyDiv[0], slot.collapseEmptyDiv[1]);
                    } else if (slot.collapseEmptyDiv.length > 0) {
                        slotObject.setCollapseEmptyDiv(slot.collapseEmptyDiv[0]);
                    }
                }

                //('dfpBind', {slot: slotObject});

                if(slotObject){
                    slotObject.addService(googletag.pubads());
                    sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setSlotObject(slotObject));
                }

                sozcuDFP.runSlot(slot);
            });
        },
        defineSlotRenderEnded: function defineSlotRenderEnded() {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
                    var slot = sozcuDFP.getSlot(event.slot.getSlotElementId());

                    if (slot) {

                        var elementContainer = sozcuCommon.querySelector('.' + event.slot.getSlotElementId() + '-container');

                        if (elementContainer) {
                            var matches = [];
                            elementContainer.classList.forEach(function (value) {
                                //remove page-parent
                                if (/^banner-size.+/.test(value)) {
                                    matches.push(value);
                                }
                            });
                            matches.forEach(function (value) {
                                elementContainer.classList.remove(value);
                            });
                        }

                        if (event.isEmpty === true) {
                            if (slot.slotRenderEndedIfIsEmptyFunctions) {
                                slot.slotRenderEndedIfIsEmptyFunctions.forEach(function (_function) {
                                    _function(event);
                                });
                            }
                        } else if (event.isEmpty === false) {
                            if (elementContainer) {
                                elementContainer.classList.add('banner-size-w-' + event.size[0]);
                                elementContainer.classList.add('banner-size-h-' + event.size[1]);
                            }

                            if (slot.slotRenderEndedIfIsNotEmptyFunctions) {
                                slot.slotRenderEndedIfIsNotEmptyFunctions.forEach(function (_function) {
                                    _function(event);
                                });
                            }

                            if (slot.slotRenderEndedIfWidthWiderFunctions) {
                                slot.slotRenderEndedIfWidthWiderFunctions.forEach(function (data) {
                                    var size = data[0];
                                    var _function = data[1];

                                    if (event.size && Array.isArray(event.size) && event.size[0] >= size) {
                                        _function(event);
                                    }
                                });
                            }

                            if (slot.slotRenderEndedIfWidthNarrowerFunctions) {
                                slot.slotRenderEndedIfWidthNarrowerFunctions.forEach(function (data) {
                                    var size = data[0];
                                    var _function = data[1];

                                    if (event.size && Array.isArray(event.size) && event.size[0] < size) {
                                        _function(event);
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
        },
        enableServices: function enableServices() {
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);
                googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
                googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad(); //googletag.pubads().enableSyncRendering();
                googletag.enableServices();
            });
        },
        getPrebidUnit: function getPrebidUnit(slot, prebidElement) {

            var bidder = null;
            if(typeof prebidElement.bidder != "undefined") {
                bidder = prebidElement.bidder;
            } else {
                console.log('Bidder not set');
                console.log(slot);
            }

            var params = null;
            if(typeof prebidElement.params != "undefined") {
                params = prebidElement.params;
            } else {
                console.log('Prebid params not set');
                console.log(slot);
            }

            var sizes = null;
            if(typeof prebidElement.sizes != "undefined") {
                sizes = prebidElement.sizes;
            } else {
                console.log('Prebid sizes not set');
                console.log(slot);
            }

            var mediaTypes = null;
            if(typeof prebidElement.mediaTypes != "undefined") {
                mediaTypes = prebidElement.mediaTypes;
            }

            var prebidUnit = null;

            if(bidder && params && sizes) {
                var prebidUnit = {
                    code: slot.adUnitPath,
                    mediaTypes: {
                        banner: {
                            sizes: sizes
                        }
                    },
                    bids: [{
                        bidder: bidder,
                        params: params
                    }]
                };

                if (mediaTypes) {
                    Object.keys(mediaTypes).forEach(function (key) {
                        prebidUnit.mediaTypes[key] = mediaTypes[key];
                    });
                }
            }

            return prebidUnit;
        },
        addPrebidAddUnits: function addPrebidAddUnits(slots, refreshForce) {
            if(!sozcuCommon.isAdvActive()){
                return false;
            }
            if (typeof refreshForce == "undefined") {
                refreshForce = false;
            }

            var adUnits = [];
            var slotAdUnitCodes = [];

            slots.forEach(function (slot) {

                if (slot.prebidData) {
                    //if (slot.prebidData && !slot.prebidInit) {
                    slot.prebidData.forEach(function (prebidElement) {
                        var unit = sozcuDFP.getPrebidUnit(slot, prebidElement);
                        if(unit) {
                            adUnits.push(unit);
                        }
                    });

                    slotAdUnitCodes.push(slot.adUnitPath);
                    //sozcuDFP.updateSlot(slot.setPrebidInit(true));
                }
            });

            if (adUnits.length) {
                pbjs.que.push(function () {
                    pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
                    var pbjsConfig = pbjsDefaultConfig;

                    pbjsConfig["currency"] = {
                        "adServerCurrency": "TRY"
                    };

                    pbjsConfig["priceGranularity"] = {
                        "buckets" : [
                            {
                                "precision": 2,
                                "min" : 0,
                                "max" : 10,
                                "increment" : 0.01
                            },
                            {
                                "precision": 2,
                                "min" : 10,
                                "max" : 25,
                                "increment" : 0.05
                            },
                            {
                                "precision": 2,
                                "min" : 25,
                                "max" : 50,
                                "increment" : 0.1
                            },
                            {
                                "precision": 2,
                                "min" : 50,
                                "max" : 100,
                                "increment" : 0.25
                            }]
                    };
                    pbjs.setConfig(pbjsConfig);
                });


                var slostsId = "";
                slots.forEach(function (slot) {
                    slostsId += slot.divId
                });

                if(
                    typeof sozcuDFP.lockGDPRPrebidInterval[slostsId] == "undefined"
                    || sozcuDFP.lockGDPRPrebidInterval[slostsId] == null
                ) {
                    sozcuDFP.lockGDPRPrebidInterval[slostsId] = setInterval(function (slots) {
                        if (!sozcuDFP.lockGDPR) {
                            var slostsId = "";
                            slots.forEach(function (slot) {
                                slostsId += slot.divId;
                                //console.log(slot.divId);
                            });

                            clearInterval(sozcuDFP.lockGDPRPrebidInterval[slostsId]);

                            pbjs.que.push(function () {
                                pbjs.requestBids({
                                    timeout: sozcuDFPConstants.preidTimeout,
                                    adUnitCodes: slotAdUnitCodes,
                                    bidsBackHandler: function bidsBackHandler() {
                                        pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync(slotAdUnitCodes);
                                        Object.keys(slots).forEach(function (key) {

                                            var slot = slots[key];
                                            sozcuDFP.refreshFunction(slot, refreshForce);
                                        });
                                    }
                                });
                            });

                        }
                    }, 10, slots);
                }

            }

        },
        addTargeting: function addTargeting(key, value) {
            sozcuDFP.targetingList[key] = value;
        },
        defineTargeting: function defineTargeting() {
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                Object.keys(sozcuDFP.targetingList).forEach(function (key) {
                    if (key && sozcuDFP.targetingList[key]) {
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting(key, sozcuDFP.targetingList[key]);
                    }
                });
            });
        },
        dfpDisplayDiv: function dfpDisplayDiv(id) {
            return '<div class="' + id + '-container dfp-container" ><div id="' + id + '" ></div></div>';
        },
        dfpDisplayScript: function dfpDisplayScript(id) {
            return '<' + 'script' + '>googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("' + id + '"); });' + '</' + 'script' + '>';
        }
    };

    <!--GDPR-->
        ( function() {
        // Run this in an interval (every 0.1s) just in case we are still waiting for consent
        var cnt = 0;
        var consentSetInterval = setInterval(function(){
            cnt += 1;
            // Bail if we have not gotten a consent response after 60 seconds.
            if( cnt === 600 )
                clearInterval(consentSetInterval);
            if( typeof window.__tcfapi !== 'undefined' ) { // Check if window.__tcfapi has been set
                clearInterval( consentSetInterval );
                window.__tcfapi( 'addEventListener', 2, function( tcData,listenerSuccess ) {
                    if ( listenerSuccess ) {
                        if( tcData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded' || tcData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete' ) {
                            var isGDPRConsent = false;
                            if ( ! tcData.gdprApplies ) {
                                // GDPR DOES NOT APPLY
                                // Insert adsbygoogle.js onto the page.
                                // insertAdsByGoogleJs();
                                console.log("No GDPR");

                            }
                            else {
                                // GDPR DOES APPLY
                                // Purpose 1 refers to the storage and/or access of information on a device.
                                var hasDeviceStorageAndAccessConsent = tcData.purpose.consents[1] || false;
                                // Google Requires Consent for Purpose 1
                                if (hasDeviceStorageAndAccessConsent) {
                                    // GLOBAL VENDOR LIST - https://iabeurope.eu/vendor-list-tcf-v2-0/
                                    // CHECK FOR GOOGLE ADVERTISING PRODUCTS CONSENT. (IAB Vendor ID 755)
                                    var hasGoogleAdvertisingProductsConsent = tcData.vendor.consents[755] || false;
                                    // Check if the user gave Google Advertising Products consent (iab vendor 755)
                                    if(hasGoogleAdvertisingProductsConsent) {
                                        // Insert adsbygoogle.js onto the page.
                                        // insertAdsByGoogleJs();
                                        isGDPRConsent = true;
                                        console.log("GDPR & Consent")
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            if(!isGDPRConsent){
                                console.log("no isGDPRConsent");
                                window.addEventListener('load',function () {
                                    if (sozcuCommon.querySelector('.ot-floating-button__front')){
                                        sozcuCommon.querySelector('.ot-floating-button__front').style.display='block';
                                    }
                                });
                                googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                                    googletag.pubads().setRequestNonPersonalizedAds(1);
                                });
                            }

                            sozcuDFP.lockGDPR = false;
                        }
                    }
                } );
            }
            cnt++;
        }, 100);
    })();
    
    <!-- END GDPR -->

    var sozcuContent = {
        onPageUrlChanged: function onPageUrlChanged() {
            sozcuContent.addIntextBanners();

        },
        onDOMContentLoaded: function onDOMContentLoaded() {
            sozcuContent.addIntextBanners();
            if(sozcuCommon.querySelector('meta[name="sgm:newsId"]')){
                var pageId = parseInt(sozcuCommon.querySelector('meta[name="sgm:newsId"]').getAttribute('content'))
                sozcuCommon.addReadArticle(pageId);
            }
        },
        addIntextBanners: function addIntextBanners() {
            if (
                !sozcuCommon.querySelector('.v3_ss_login_true')
                &&
                !(
                    sozcuCommon.querySelectorAll('.main-detail .news-cat a').length > 1
                    && sozcuCommon.querySelectorAll('.main-detail .news-cat a')[1].href.indexOf('/kategori/ilan-2') > -1
                )
            ) {
                var max_adv = 3;
                var heightThreshold;

                if (sozcuCommon.isMobile()) {
                    heightThreshold = sozcuDFPConstants.intextHeightMobileThreshold;
                    max_adv = 5;

                    if (sozcuCommon.querySelector('.columnist-detail .author-the-content')) {
                        max_adv = 3;
                    }

                } else {
                    heightThreshold = sozcuDFPConstants.intextHeightDesktopThreshold;
                } //Max limit for inner adv


                var countSlots = 0;

                sozcuCommon.querySelectorAll('.content-element').forEach(function (node) {
                    var contentElementBounding = node.getBoundingClientRect();

                    if (!sozcuCommon.querySelector(".contentInnerAdv", node)) {
                        var contentTotalHeight = contentElementBounding.height;
                        var lastOffsetTop = 0;

                        if (node.children) {

                            var topChild = null;

                            for (var i = 0; i < node.children.length; i++) {
                                var childNode = node.children[i];
                                var childNodeBounding = childNode.getBoundingClientRect();
                                var bdBnnrCnt = sozcuCommon.querySelectorAll(".contentInnerAdv").length + 1;
                                var offsetInnerTop = childNodeBounding.top - contentElementBounding.top;

                                if (offsetInnerTop - lastOffsetTop > heightThreshold) {
                                    if (childNode.tagName == 'P'
                                        && childNode.innerHTML.length > 200
                                        && childNode.querySelectorAll('img').length===0
                                        && !(topChild && topChild.tagName == 'H2')
                                        && !(topChild && topChild.tagName == 'P' && topChild.firstElementChild && topChild.firstElementChild.tagName == "STRONG")
                                    ) {
                                        if (contentTotalHeight - offsetInnerTop < 300) {
                                            return false;
                                        }

                                        lastOffsetTop = offsetInnerTop; // --- DFP Block

                                        var divId = "sozcu_content_area_load" + bdBnnrCnt;

                                        if (sozcuCommon.isMobile()) {
                                            var adUnitPath = '/66738120/sozcu_body_intext_mobile';
                                            if(bdBnnrCnt == 1){
                                                var adUnitPath = '/66738120/sozcu_body_intext_mobile_first';
                                                divId = 'sozcu_body_intext_mobile_first';
                                            }

                                            sozcuDFP.addSlot(
                                                sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot()
                                                    .setAdUnitPath(adUnitPath)
                                                    .setDivId(divId)
                                                    .setSizes([[300, 250], [1, 1], [200, 200], [250, 250], [300, 50], [300, 100], [320, 50], [320, 100], [336, 280], 'fluid'])
                                                    .setPrebidData(sozcuPrebidData_300_250)
                                                    .addPrebidData({bidder: 'adform', params: { mid: 567290 }, sizes: [[300, 250]]})
                                            );
                                            if (country != 'tr'){
                                                sozcuDFP.updateSlot(sozcuDFP.getSlot(divId)
                                                    .addPrebidData({bidder: 'improvedigital', params: { placementId: 22379773}, sizes: [[300, 250]]}));
                                            }

                                        } else {
                                            var adUnitPath = '/66738120/sozcu_body_intext_300x250';
                                            if(bdBnnrCnt == 1){
                                                var adUnitPath = '/66738120/sozcu_body_intext_300x250_first';
                                                divId = 'sozcu_body_intext_300x250_first';
                                            }
                                            sozcuDFP.addSlot(
                                                sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot()
                                                    .setAdUnitPath(adUnitPath)
                                                    .setDivId(divId)
                                                    .setSizes([[300, 250], [1, 1], [200, 200], [250, 250], [336, 280], 'fluid'])
                                                    .setPrebidData(sozcuPrebidData_300_250)
                                                    .addPrebidData({bidder: 'adform', params: { mid: 563080 }, sizes: [[300, 250]]})
                                            );

                                            if (country != 'tr'){
                                                sozcuDFP.updateSlot(sozcuDFP.getSlot(divId)
                                                    .addPrebidData({bidder: 'improvedigital', params: { placementId: 22379755}, sizes: [[300, 250]]}));
                                            }

                                        }

                                        childNode.insertAdjacentHTML("beforebegin",  '<div class="contentInnerAdv" style="float:right;margin-bottom:20px;">' + sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayDiv(divId) + '</div>');

                                        countSlots++;

                                        if (max_adv !== null) {
                                            max_adv = max_adv - 1;

                                            if (max_adv <= 0) {
                                                return false;
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                topChild = childNode;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });

                if (countSlots > 0) {
                    sozcuDFP.init();
                }
            }
        },
        defineNativoSlots: function defineNativoSlots(bdBnnrCnt) {
            var start = arguments.length > 1 && arguments[1] !== undefined ? arguments[1] : 0;
            var divIdn1 = "nativo" + (1 + start) + "_load" + bdBnnrCnt;
            var divIdn2 = "nativo" + (2 + start) + "_load" + bdBnnrCnt;
            var divIdn3 = "nativo" + (3 + start) + "_load" + bdBnnrCnt;
            sozcuDFP.addSlot(sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot().setAdUnitPath('/66738120/nativo' + (1 + start)).setDivId(divIdn1).setSizes(["fluid"]));
            sozcuDFP.addSlot(sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot().setAdUnitPath('/66738120/nativo' + (2 + start)).setDivId(divIdn2).setSizes(["fluid"]));
            sozcuDFP.addSlot(sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot().setAdUnitPath('/66738120/nativo' + (3 + start)).setDivId(divIdn3).setSizes(["fluid"]));
            var addMobile = '';
            if(bdBnnrCnt.toString().indexOf('mobil_four') !== -1){
                var divIdn4 = "nativo" + (4 + start) + "_load" + bdBnnrCnt;
                sozcuDFP.addSlot(sozcuDFP.getSozcuDFPSlot().setAdUnitPath('/66738120/nativo' + (4 + start)).setDivId(divIdn4).setSizes(["fluid"]));
                addMobile = sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayDiv(divIdn4);
            }
            var htmlNativo = '<div class="nativo-inner">' + sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayDiv(divIdn1) + sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayDiv(divIdn2) + sozcuDFP.dfpDisplayDiv(divIdn3) + addMobile  + '</div>';
            return htmlNativo;
        }
    };

        sozcuContent.onDOMContentLoaded();

    window.addEventListener('load',function () {
        var uaParser = new UAParser();
        if(uaParser.getBrowser().name!=='Chrome' && ((uaParser.getOS().name==='iOS' && parseInt(uaParser.getOS().version) <= 9) || (uaParser.getOS().name==='Android' && parseInt(uaParser.getOS().version) <= 7))){
            document.getElementsByClassName('content-head')[0].classList.add('dblock');
        }

    (function (window, undefined) {

        'use strict';

        //////////////
        // Constants
        /////////////


        var LIBVERSION  = '0.7.19',
            EMPTY       = '',
            UNKNOWN     = '?',
            FUNC_TYPE   = 'function',
            UNDEF_TYPE  = 'undefined',
            OBJ_TYPE    = 'object',
            STR_TYPE    = 'string',
            MAJOR       = 'major', // deprecated
            MODEL       = 'model',
            NAME        = 'name',
            TYPE        = 'type',
            VENDOR      = 'vendor',
            VERSION     = 'version',
            ARCHITECTURE= 'architecture',
            CONSOLE     = 'console',
            MOBILE      = 'mobile',
            TABLET      = 'tablet',
            SMARTTV     = 'smarttv',
            WEARABLE    = 'wearable',
            EMBEDDED    = 'embedded';


        ///////////
        // Helper
        //////////


        var util = {
            extend : function (regexes, extensions) {
                var margedRegexes = {};
                for (var i in regexes) {
                    if (extensions[i] && extensions[i].length % 2 === 0) {
                        margedRegexes[i] = extensions[i].concat(regexes[i]);
                    } else {
                        margedRegexes[i] = regexes[i];
                    }
                }
                return margedRegexes;
            },
            has : function (str1, str2) {
                if (typeof str1 === "string") {
                    return str2.toLowerCase().indexOf(str1.toLowerCase()) !== -1;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            },
            lowerize : function (str) {
                return str.toLowerCase();
            },
            major : function (version) {
                return typeof(version) === STR_TYPE ? version.replace(/[^\d\.]/g,'').split(".")[0] : undefined;
            },
            trim : function (str) {
                return str.replace(/^[\s\uFEFF\xA0]+|[\s\uFEFF\xA0]+$/g, '');
            }
        };


        ///////////////
        // Map helper
        //////////////


        var mapper = {

            rgx : function (ua, arrays) {

                //var result = {},
                var i = 0, j, k, p, q, matches, match;//, args = arguments;

                /*// construct object barebones
                for (p = 0; p < args[1].length; p++) {
                    q = args[1][p];
                    result[typeof q === OBJ_TYPE ? q[0] : q] = undefined;
                }*/

                // loop through all regexes maps
                while (i < arrays.length && !matches) {

                    var regex = arrays[i],       // even sequence (0,2,4,..)
                        props = arrays[i + 1];   // odd sequence (1,3,5,..)
                    j = k = 0;

                    // try matching uastring with regexes
                    while (j < regex.length && !matches) {

                        matches = regex[j++].exec(ua);

                        if (!!matches) {
                            for (p = 0; p < props.length; p++) {
                                match = matches[++k];
                                q = props[p];
                                // check if given property is actually array
                                if (typeof q === OBJ_TYPE && q.length > 0) {
                                    if (q.length == 2) {
                                        if (typeof q[1] == FUNC_TYPE) {
                                            // assign modified match
                                            this[q[0]] = q[1].call(this, match);
                                        } else {
                                            // assign given value, ignore regex match
                                            this[q[0]] = q[1];
                                        }
                                    } else if (q.length == 3) {
                                        // check whether function or regex
                                        if (typeof q[1] === FUNC_TYPE && !(q[1].exec && q[1].test)) {
                                            // call function (usually string mapper)
                                            this[q[0]] = match ? q[1].call(this, match, q[2]) : undefined;
                                        } else {
                                            // sanitize match using given regex
                                            this[q[0]] = match ? match.replace(q[1], q[2]) : undefined;
                                        }
                                    } else if (q.length == 4) {
                                        this[q[0]] = match ? q[3].call(this, match.replace(q[1], q[2])) : undefined;
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    this[q] = match ? match : undefined;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    i += 2;
                }
                //return this;
            },

            str : function (str, map) {

                for (var i in map) {
                    // check if array
                    if (typeof map[i] === OBJ_TYPE && map[i].length > 0) {
                        for (var j = 0; j < map[i].length; j++) {
                            if (util.has(map[i][j], str)) {
                                return (i === UNKNOWN) ? undefined : i;
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (util.has(map[i], str)) {
                        return (i === UNKNOWN) ? undefined : i;
                    }
                }
                return str;
            }
        };


        ///////////////
        // String map
        //////////////


        var maps = {

            browser : {
                oldsafari : {
                    version : {
                        '1.0'   : '/8',
                        '1.2'   : '/1',
                        '1.3'   : '/3',
                        '2.0'   : '/412',
                        '2.0.2' : '/416',
                        '2.0.3' : '/417',
                        '2.0.4' : '/419',
                        '?'     : '/'
                    }
                }
            },

            device : {
                amazon : {
                    model : {
                        'Fire Phone' : ['SD', 'KF']
                    }
                },
                sprint : {
                    model : {

                    vendor : {

                        'Sprint'    : 'Sprint'

            os : {
                windows : {

                        'NT 3.11'   : 'NT3.51',
                        'NT 4.0'    : 'NT4.0',
                        '2000'      : 'NT 5.0',
                        'XP'        : ['NT 5.1', 'NT 5.2'],
                        'Vista'     : 'NT 6.0',

        /////////////////
        // Constructor
        ////////////////
        /*
        var Browser = function (name, version) {
            this[NAME] = name;
            this[VERSION] = version;
        };
        var CPU = function (arch) {
            this[ARCHITECTURE] = arch;
        };
        var Device = function (vendor, model, type) {
            this[VENDOR] = vendor;
            this[MODEL] = model;
            this[TYPE] = type;
        };
        var Engine = Browser;
        var OS = Browser;
        */
        var UAParser = function (uastring, extensions) {

            if (typeof uastring === 'object') {
                extensions = uastring;
                uastring = undefined;
            }

            if (!(this instanceof UAParser)) {
                return new UAParser(uastring, extensions).getResult();
            }

            var ua = uastring || ((window && window.navigator && window.navigator.userAgent) ? window.navigator.userAgent : EMPTY);
            var rgxmap = extensions ? util.extend(regexes, extensions) : regexes;
            //var browser = new Browser();
            //var cpu = new CPU();
            //var device = new Device();
            //var engine = new Engine();
            //var os = new OS();

            this.getBrowser = function () {
                var browser = { name: undefined, version: undefined };
                mapper.rgx.call(browser, ua, rgxmap.browser);
                browser.major = util.major(browser.version); // deprecated
                return browser;
            };
            this.getCPU = function () {
                var cpu = { architecture: undefined };
                mapper.rgx.call(cpu, ua, rgxmap.cpu);
                return cpu;
            };
            this.getDevice = function () {
                var device = { vendor: undefined, model: undefined, type: undefined };
                mapper.rgx.call(device, ua, rgxmap.device);
                return device;
            };
            this.getEngine = function () {
                var engine = { name: undefined, version: undefined };
                mapper.rgx.call(engine, ua, rgxmap.engine);
                return engine;
            };
            this.getOS = function () {
                var os = { name: undefined, version: undefined };
                mapper.rgx.call(os, ua, rgxmap.os);
                return os;
            };
            this.getResult = function () {
                return {
                    ua      : this.getUA(),
                    browser : this.getBrowser(),
                    engine  : this.getEngine(),
                    os      : this.getOS(),
                    device  : this.getDevice(),
                    cpu     : this.getCPU()
                };
            };
            this.getUA = function () {
                return ua;
            };
            this.setUA = function (uastring) {
                ua = uastring;
                //browser = new Browser();
                //cpu = new CPU();
                //device = new Device();
                //engine = new Engine();
                //os = new OS();
                return this;
            };
            return this;
        };

        UAParser.VERSION = LIBVERSION;
        UAParser.BROWSER = {
            NAME    : NAME,
            MAJOR   : MAJOR, // deprecated
            VERSION : VERSION
        };
        UAParser.CPU = {
            ARCHITECTURE : ARCHITECTURE
        };
        UAParser.DEVICE = {
            MODEL   : MODEL,
            VENDOR  : VENDOR,
            TYPE    : TYPE,
            CONSOLE : CONSOLE,
            MOBILE  : MOBILE,
            SMARTTV : SMARTTV,
            TABLET  : TABLET,
            WEARABLE: WEARABLE,
            EMBEDDED: EMBEDDED
        };
        UAParser.ENGINE = {
            NAME    : NAME,
            VERSION : VERSION
        };
        UAParser.OS = {
            NAME    : NAME,
            VERSION : VERSION
        };
        //UAParser.Utils = util;

        ///////////
        // Export
        //////////

        // check js environment
        if (typeof(exports) !== UNDEF_TYPE) {
            // nodejs env
            if (typeof module !== UNDEF_TYPE && module.exports) {
                exports = module.exports = UAParser;
            }
            // TODO: test!!!!!!!!
            /*
            if (require && require.main === module && process) {
                // cli
                var jsonize = function (arr) {
                    var res = [];
                    for (var i in arr) {
                        res.push(new UAParser(arr[i]).getResult());
                    }
                    process.stdout.write(jsHelper.jsonStringify(res, null, 2) + '\n');
                };
                if (process.stdin.isTTY) {
                    // via args
                    jsonize(process.argv.slice(2));
                } else {
                    // via pipe
                    var str = '';
                    process.stdin.on('readable', functi

                        var read = process.stdin.read();

                            str += read;
                        }
                    });
                    process.stdin.on('end', function () {
                        jsonize(str.replace(/\n$/, '').split('\n'));
                    });
                }
            }
            */
            exports.UAParser = UAParser;
        } else {
            // requirejs env (optional)
            if (typeof(define) === FUNC_TYPE && define.amd) {
                define(function () {
                    return UAParser;
                });
            } else if (window) {
                // browser env
                window.UAParser = UAParser;
            }
        }

        // jQuery/Zepto specific (optional)
        // Note:
        //   In AMD env the global scope should be kept clean, but jQuery is an exception.
        //   jQuery always exports to global scope, unless jQuery.noConflict(true) is used,
        //   and we should catch that.
        var $ = window && (window.jQuery || window.Zepto);
        if (typeof $ !== UNDEF_TYPE && !$.ua) {
            var parser = new UAParser();
            $.ua = parser.getResult();
            $.ua.get = function () {
                return parser.getUA();
            };
            $.ua.set = function (uastring) {
                parser.setUA(uastring);
                var result = parser.getResult();
                for (var prop in result) {
                    $.ua[prop] = result[prop];
                }
            };
        }

    })(typeof window === 'object' ? window : this);
